    (function(win){if (win.tgtElemReady===undefined){win.adobeListeners=[]; var doc=win.document, MutationObserver=win.MutationObserver || win.WebKitMutationObserver, observer; function isElementNotInArray(element){if (win.adobeListeners.length===0){return true;}else{for (var i=0, len=win.adobeListeners.length; i < len; i++){if (win.adobeListeners[i].selector===element){return false;}}return true;}}function tgtElemReady(selector, fn, campaignName){var elementInArray=isElementNotInArray(selector); if (elementInArray){win.adobeListeners.push({selector: selector, fn: fn, campaign: campaignName});}if (!observer){observer=new MutationObserver(check); observer.observe(doc.documentElement,{childList: true, subtree: true, attributes: true});}check();}function check(){for (var i=0, len=win.adobeListeners.length, listener, elements; i < len; i++){listener=win.adobeListeners[i]; elements=doc.querySelectorAll(listener.selector); for (var j=0, jLen=elements.length, element; j < jLen; j++){element=elements[j]; if (!element.ready){element.ready=true; listener.fn.call(element, element);}}}}win.tgtElemReady=tgtElemReady;}})(this);

            exSizeMobile: "85%", // specify percentage reduction for mobile view
            exColor: "#000000",
            exURL: "https://www.macys.com/shop",
            addToLine: "", // use 1, 2, 3, etc or leave blank

            // link full cdt container
            fullCDTLink: "/shop/sale/Price_discount_range/20_PERCENT_%20off%20%26%20more?id=3536" // add url here (or leave blank)

            deadline: '01/02/2023 23:59:00',
            dayLightSavingsStart: "2022/03/13 02:00:00 PST", // Put the start date for Daylight Saving

            addTextLines: function() {
                this.classList.add("adobeCDTcontain");

                if(document.querySelectorAll("#tntbanner").length > 0){
                    document.querySelectorAll("#tntbanner").remove();
                }

                        var convertToString = convertToEmValue.toString() + "em";
                        lineNum.style.fontSize = convertToString;
                        lineNum.style.color=textLines['color'+j];
                    }

                var numLinesInt = parseFloat(textLines.addToLine);

                if (numLinesInt === "" || numLinesInt === null || numLinesInt === undefined) {
                    // do nothing if blank
                }
                else if (numLinesInt > 0) {
                    document.querySelector('[id*="adobeHTMLLine' + numLinesInt + '"]').insertAdjacentHTML("beforeEnd", injMbox.exElement);

            calcFonts: function(breakPoint) {
                if (numberOfLines > 0) {
                    for (var j = 1; j <= numberOfLines; j++) {
                        var adobeLine = 'adobeHTMLLine' + j;
                        var lineNum = document.getElementById(adobeLine);
                        lineNum.style.fontSize=textLines['size'+j];
                        var getFontSize = textLines['size'+j];
                        var convertToEmValue = "";
                        if(breakPoint === "mobile") {
                            // reduce em font size to 52% of desktop font size
                            var convertToEmValue = ( parseFloat(getFontSize) / 16 ) * .78;
                        }
                        else if (breakPoint === "desktop") {
                            var convertToEmValue = parseFloat(getFontSize) / 16;
                        }

                        var convertToString = convertToEmValue.toString() + "em";
                        lineNum.style.fontSize = convertToString;
                    }
                }

                // check and update exclusions font
                var getExcFont = textLines.exSize;
                var getExcFontMobPercentRaw = textLines.exSizeMobile;
                var excToEmVal = "";
                var parentLineSize = "";
                var sizeOfExcLine = textLines['size'+textLines.addToLine];
                if(sizeOfExcLine === "" || sizeOfExcLine === " " || sizeOfExcLine === null || sizeOfExcLine === undefined) {
                    // do nothing if exclusions are not added
                }
                else {
                    // update the exclusions font size in a relative and dynamic way 
                    if(breakPoint === "mobile") {
                        // reduce em font size based on percent specified
                        var excToEmVal = ( parseFloat(getExcFont) / parseFloat(sizeOfExcLine) ) * ( parseFloat(getExcFontMobPercentRaw) / 100);
                    }
                    else if (breakPoint === "desktop") {
                        // var excToEmVal = parseFloat(getExcFont) / 16;
                        var excToEmVal = parseFloat(getExcFont) / parseFloat(sizeOfExcLine);
                    }
                    var excToString = excToEmVal.toString() + "em";
                    document.getElementById("tnt_exclusionsText").style.fontSize = excToString;
                    // document.getElementById("tntExclusionsURL").style.fontSize = excToString;
                }
            },

            CDTlinking: function() {
                var fullLink = textLines.fullCDTLink;
                if (fullLink === null || fullLink === undefined || fullLink === "" || fullLink === "") {
                    // do nothing if textLines.fullCDTLink is empty
                }
                else {
                    // add href value if textLines.fullCDTLink is set
                    document.getElementById('CDTLink').href = fullLink;
                }
            },

            adjustFonts: function() {
                var docWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
                var mobOrDesk = "";
                if(docWidth <= 800) {
                    var mobOrDesk = "mobile"; 
                }
                else {
                    var mobOrDesk = "desktop";
                }
                injMbox.calcFonts(mobOrDesk);
            },

            initClock: function() { //create CM tag
                injMbox.initializeClock('clockdiv', injMbox.deadline);
            },

            getTimeRemaining: function(endtime) {
                var t = Date.parse(endtime) - Date.parse(new Date());
                var seconds = Math.floor((t / 1000) % 60);
                var minutes = Math.floor((t / 1000 / 60) % 60);
                var hours = Math.floor(t / (1000 * 60 * 60));
                var todayDate = new Date();
                var ds1 = new Date(injMbox.dayLightSavingsStart);
                var ds2 = new Date(injMbox.dayLightSavingsEnd);

                return {
                    'total': t,
                    'hours': hours,
                    'minutes': minutes,
                    'seconds': seconds
                };
            },


            initializeClock: function(id, endtime) {
                var deadLine = "";
                var clock = document.getElementById(id);
                var hoursSpan = clock.querySelector('.hours');
                var minutesSpan = clock.querySelector('.minutes');
                var secondsSpan = clock.querySelector('.seconds');

                var todayStr = endtime;
                var today = new Date(todayStr);
                Date.prototype.stdTimezoneOffset = function() {
                    var jan = new Date(this.getFullYear(), 0, 1);
                    var jul = new Date(this.getFullYear(), 6, 1);
                    return Math.max(jan.getTimezoneOffset(), jul.getTimezoneOffset());
                };
                Date.prototype.dst = function() {
                    return this.getTimezoneOffset() < this.stdTimezoneOffset();
                };
                if (today.dst()) {
                    deadLine = todayStr + ' GMT-0700';
                    //console.log("Daylight savings time!" + deadLine);
                } else {
                    deadLine = todayStr + ' GMT-0800';
                    //console.log("Not Daylight savings time!" + deadLine);
                }

                function updateClock() {
                    var t = injMbox.getTimeRemaining(deadLine);
                    //console.log("Final Time" + t.hours);

                    hoursSpan.innerHTML = (t.hours);
                    minutesSpan.innerHTML = ('0' + t.minutes).slice(-2);
                    secondsSpan.innerHTML = ('0' + t.seconds).slice(-2);

                    if (t.total <= 0) {
                        clearInterval(timeinterval);
                        console.log("Time passed for clock timer");
                        document.getElementById('tntbanner').remove();
                    }
                }

                updateClock();
                var timeinterval = setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
            },

            check: function() {
              tgtElemReady('.mainContainer:first-of-type', injMbox.addTextLines, 'PROD_CDT_ODS_01_02_2023'); 
              tgtElemReady('.mainContainer:first-of-type #canvas > div[id^="row"]:first-of-type', injMbox.addTextLines, 'PROD_CDT_ODS_01_02_2023');

                tgtElemReady('#mainContent > .product-details-feature', injMbox.addTextLines, 'PROD_CDT_ODS_01_02_2023');
                tgtElemReady('#mainCont > .pdp', injMbox.addTextLines, 'PROD_CDT_ODS_01_02_2023');
            }
        };

        //Call the check function
       try {
            injMbox.check();
       } catch (e) {
           throw e.toString();
       }

    })();

The information collected might relate to you, your preferences or your device, and is mostly used to make the site work as you expect it to and to provide a more personalized web experience. However, you can choose not to allow certain types of cookies, which may impact your experience of the site and the services we are able to offer. Click on the different category headings to find out more and change our default settings according to your preference.
                <br><a href="https://customerservice-macys.com/articles/macys-and-macyscom-notice-of-privacy-practices#Cookies" class="privacy-notice-link" rel="noopener" target="_blank" aria-label="More information about your privacy, opens in a new tab">More information</a></p></div></li><li class="ot-cat-item ot-always-active-group" role="presentation" data-optanongroupid="C0001"><div class="category-menu-switch-handler" role="tab" tabindex="-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0001"><h3 id="ot-header-id-C0001">Strictly Necessary Cookies</h3></div><div class="ot-desc-cntr ot-hide ot-always-active-group" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0" id="ot-desc-id-C0001"><div class="ot-grp-hdr1"><h4 class="ot-cat-header">Strictly Necessary Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl-cntr"><div class="ot-always-active">Always Active</div></div></div><p class="ot-grp-desc ot-category-desc">These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personal information.</p></div></li><li class="ot-cat-item ot-always-active-group" role="presentation" data-optanongroupid="C0003"><div class="category-menu-switch-handler" role="tab" tabindex="-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0003"><h3 id="ot-header-id-C0003">Functional Cookies</h3></div><div class="ot-desc-cntr ot-hide ot-always-active-group" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0" id="ot-desc-id-C0003"><div class="ot-grp-hdr1"><h4 class="ot-cat-header">Functional Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl-cntr"><div class="ot-always-active">Always Active</div></div></div><p class="ot-grp-desc ot-category-desc">These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalization. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages.You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but then some or all of these services may not function properly.</p></div></li><li class="ot-cat-item ot-always-active-group" role="presentation" data-optanongroupid="C0002"><div class="category-menu-switch-handler" role="tab" tabindex="-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0002"><h3 id="ot-header-id-C0002">Performance Cookies</h3></div><div class="ot-desc-cntr ot-hide ot-always-active-group" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0" id="ot-desc-id-C0002"><div class="ot-grp-hdr1"><h4 class="ot-cat-header">Performance Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl-cntr"><div class="ot-always-active">Always Active</div></div></div><p class="ot-grp-desc ot-category-desc">These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous.You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but then we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.</p></div></li><li class="ot-cat-item" role="presentation" data-optanongroupid="SPD_BG"><div class="category-menu-switch-handler" role="tab" tabindex="-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-SPD_BG"><h3 id="ot-header-id-SPD_BG">Sale of Personal Information</h3></div><div class="ot-desc-cntr ot-hide" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0" id="ot-desc-id-SPD_BG"><div class="ot-grp-hdr1"><h4 class="ot-cat-header">Sale of Personal Information</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-SPD_BG" id="ot-group-id-SPD_BG" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="SPD_BG" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-SPD_BG"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-SPD_BG"><span class="ot-switch-nob"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Sale of Personal Information</span></label> </div><div class="ot-tgl-cntr"></div></div><p class="ot-grp-desc ot-category-desc">These cookies collect information for analytics and to personalize your experience with targeted ads.
